# 3D Gaussian Splatting Papers

## рҹ“ў ж”№зүҲе…¬е‘Ҡ / Update Notice

з”ұдәҺи®әж–Үж•°йҮҸжҝҖеўһпјҢйЎөйқўеҸҳеҫ—иҝҮй•ҝгҖӮдёәж–№дҫҝжҹҘйҳ…пјҢжҲ‘д»¬е°Ҷ2024е№ҙ6жңҲд№ӢеүҚзҡ„и®әж–ҮжҡӮж—¶[рҹ“Ғ еҪ’жЎЈ](https://github.com/Awesome3DGS/3D-Gaussian-Splatting-Papers/tree/archive/202406)пјҲеҗҺз»ӯиҝӣдёҖжӯҘж•ҙзҗҶпјүпјҢе№¶жҠҠжңҖж–°и®әж–Үи°ғж•ҙдёәжҢүж—¶й—ҙеҖ’еәҸжҺ’еҲ—гҖӮ

Due to the rapid increase in the number of papers, the page has become too long.
To facilitate the review, we have temporarily
[рҹ“Ғ archived](https://github.com/Awesome3DGS/3D-Gaussian-Splatting-Papers/tree/archive/202406) papers
before Jan 2024 (which will be further organized) and rearranged latest papers
in reverse chronological order.

[![жҸҗдәӨдҝ®ж”№](https://img.shields.io/badge/рҹ‘җ-жҸҗдәӨдҝ®ж”№-brightgreen.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/Awesome3DGS/3D-Gaussian-Splatting-Papers/pulls)
